     &lt;!--

    function showDetails2(itemnum) {
        alert(itemnum);
        document.getElementById('weekly1').style.position = "static";
        document.getElementById('weekly1').style.visibility = "visible";

    }


    function getQSValue(url, name) {

        var temp;
        var tokens = [];
        var subtokens = []

        temp = url;

        try {
            tokens = temp.split("&amp;");

            for (var i = 0; i &lt; tokens.length; i++) {
                subtokens = tokens[i].split("=");
                if (subtokens[0] === name) {
                    return subtokens[1];
                }
            }
        } catch (e) {
        }
    }
    var counter = 1;
    var tracker = 1;

    $(function() {

        $.ajaxSetup({ cache: false });

        var dlg;

        $('.eyeball').on('click', function(e) {

            var pvID;
            e.preventDefault();

            var qs = $(this).next().attr('href')
            pvID = getQSValue(qs, 'bo_products_variance_id');
            $.get('/checkout/Details_Popup.asp',
                { bo_websiteconfig_id: '1',
                    bo_products_variance_id: pvID,
                    callback: 'b'
                }).done(function(data) {
                    $('#dialogDetails').html(data);
                    $("#dialogDetails").dialog({
                        modal: false,
                        autoOpen: false,
                        height: 500,
                        draggable: false,
                        width: 800,
                        closeText: 'hide'
                    });
                    $('#dialogDetails').dialog('open');

                    //initialize hooks
                    tracker = $('.slider a').length;
                    counter = 1;

                    $('#previous').on('click', function(e) {
                        e.preventDefault();

                        if (counter === 1) {
                            return;
                        } else {
                            counter--;
                        }

                        $('.slider').animate({ 'margin-left': '+=300px' });
                    });

                    $('#next').on('click', function(e) {
                        e.preventDefault();
                        if (tracker === counter) {
                            return;
                        } else {
                            counter++;
                        }
                        $('.slider').animate({ 'margin-left': '-=300px' });
                    });


                    $('a.resultsPopupThumbnailLink').on('click', function(e) {
                        e.preventDefault();
                        counter = $(this).index() + 1;
                        var moveBy = $(this).index();
                        $('.slider').css('margin-left', '0px');
                        $('.slider').css('margin-left', '-=' + (moveBy * 300).toString());

                    });

                });
        });
    });
	
	$(document).ready(function() {
		$(".resultsItemIMG").on('mouseover', function() {
			// For Sold Out Items : No Cart Button &gt; No Eyeball
			if( $(this).closest(".resultsItemWrapper").find(".cartButton").length &gt; 0 )
			{
				$(this).find(".eyeball").show();
			}
		});
		$(".resultsItemIMG").on('mouseout', function() {
			$(this).find(".eyeball").hide();
		});
	});

//--&gt;
    </script>
